Unlike question-answering-based evaluation of cinematic understanding, cinematographic captioning requires a unified open-form description over multiple cinematographic dimensions. This task is challenging for two main reasons: the model must infer professional cinematographic concepts from subtle visual evidence, and it must generate captions that are both comprehensive and accurate. Accordingly, we propose CineCap, a framework that combines structured reasoning with spatio-temporal anchors and reinforcement learning with comprehensiveness, accuracy, and gated coverage rewards. The former grounds professional cinematographic descriptions in explicit visual evidence and organizes them into compact atomic reasoning for supervised fine-tuning, while the latter improves the balance between descriptive completeness and factual correctness. In addition, we construct CineCap Bench, a benchmark of 472 manually annotated video-caption pairs for systematic evaluation. Extensive experiments show that CineCap consistently outperforms strong proprietary and open-source baselines, establishing a new state of the art for cinematographic captioning. ### [246] [Decentralised AI Training and Inference with BlockTrain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24722)
*Peter Toth*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Spheroid BlockTrain，一种去中心化的模型训练协议，将模型拆分为独立可训练的块，每个块在全局目标下进行本地优化，推理时组合成一个完整模型。在字节级WikiText上达到CE 1.359（困惑度3.89），接近端到端Transformer基线（CE差约0.04），且每个worker只训练一个块，无需完整优化器状态。分布式训练（6个worker）通过平均相同块的更新达到CE 1.385。实际HTTP/TCP传输实验验证了序列化检查点和更新的传输可行性，包括公有IP三主机运行将CE从5.580提升至1.811，传输15.22 GB数据。推理时采用单次块栈遍历生成完整输出，通过直接TCP在三个公有网络GPU主机上支持高达75.80B参数的逻辑fp16模型，优于普通自回归TCP流水线基线（因其每次WAN流水线遍历生成完整序列而非单个token）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前前沿AI训练越来越依赖于密集、集中控制的加速器集群，这为超大规模企业和大型集中实验室带来了结构性优势，使得开放或独立的人工智能研究受限于稀缺资本、特权基础设施和数据中心地理位置。去中心化训练协议旨在打破这种集中化垄断，降低独立研究者的参与门槛。

Method: 将模型分割为独立可训练块（blocks），每个块在全局目标的局部优化目标下独立训练，推理时组合为完整模型。每个worker只训练一个块，避免完整优化器状态。通过平均相同块的更新实现分布式训练。使用HTTP/TCP传输序列化检查点和更新，推理时采用一次块栈遍历生成完整输出序列。

Result: 字节级WikiText上CE 1.359（困惑度3.89），接近基线（差约0.04 CE）。6-worker分布式训练达到CE 1.385。公有IP三主机运行将CE从5.580提升至1.811，传输15.22 GB。推理支持75.80B参数逻辑fp16模型，优于自回归TCP流水线基线。

Conclusion: BlockTrain通过去中心化的块训练协议，在不牺牲太多模型质量的前提下，实现了低资源环境下的模型训练和推理，为开放和独立AI研究提供了一种可行的去中心化替代方案。

Abstract: Frontier AI training is increasingly shaped by access to dense, centrally controlled accelerator clusters. This creates a structural advantage for hyperscalers and large centralized laboratories, and makes open or independent AI efforts depend on scarce capital, privileged infrastructure, and data-center geography. We present Spheroid BlockTrain, a decentralized training protocol in which a model is partitioned into independently trainable blocks, each optimized on a local objective derived from the same global target and composed at inference into one model. On byte-level WikiText, BlockTrain reaches cross entropy 1.359 (perplexity 3.89), within about 0.04 CE of a same-setup end-to-end Transformer reference, while each active worker trains only one block and avoids full-model optimizer state. A shared six-worker block training run reaches CE 1.385 by averaging same-block updates into one assembled model. HTTP/TCP transport experiments move real serialized checkpoints and updates, including a public-IP three-host run that improves CE from 5.580 to 1.811 while moving 15.22 GB. For inference, the current BlockTrain path uses one block-stack traversal per full output and serves over direct TCP across three public-network GPU hosts up to a 75.80B-parameter logical fp16 shape, outperforming a matched plain-autoregressive TCP pipeline baseline because it emits a full sequence per WAN pipeline traversal rather than one token per traversal.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以量化金融为应用领域，比较logit-based和LoRA-based蒸馏方法在迭代结构剪枝下的表现，并提出混合链式思维监督损失来稳定推理轨迹上的KL散度蒸馏。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve strong performance across a growing range of domains, yet their scale poses deployment challenges in applications where latency and cost constraints are critical. Using quantitative finance as our application domain, we compare logit-based and LoRA-based distillation under iterative structural pruning, introducing a blended chain-of-thought supervision loss that stabilizes KL-divergence distillation over reasoning traces. In-domain task quality degrades predictably under compression while general-knowledge benchmarks collapse well before the same point; supervision format is the key driver of this tradeoff, with chain-of-thought supervision actively recovering general knowledge that pruning erases. We release the headline dataset FinHeadlineMix, scaling law results, and practical recommendations to provide a reusable framework for domain-specific compression decisions.

### [248] [Can Scale Save Us From Plasticity Loss in Large Language Models?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24752)
*J. Fernando Hernandez-Garcia,Tomás Figliolia,Beren Millidge*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了Transformer-based LLM在持续学习中的可塑性丧失问题，发现模型（5M-314M参数）在越南语探测任务上出现性能退化，且可塑性丧失遵循随模型规模亚线性增长的标度律。更大的模型能延缓但无法完全避免该问题，且在稳态多语言训练下也存在可塑性丧失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可塑性丧失（loss of plasticity）是神经网络持续学习中的基本挑战，但已有研究多集中在较老的小型架构上，且很少涉及自然语言领域。本文旨在验证该问题是否在现代基于Transformer的LLM范式中仍然存在。

Method: 在GPT风格Transformer模型（5M-314M非嵌入参数）上进行多语言持续学习实验，通过越南语保留探测任务的性能退化来度量可塑性丧失，并分析其与模型规模的标度关系。

Result: 1) 所有规模模型均出现可塑性丧失；2) 可塑性丧失遵循随模型规模亚线性增长的标度律；3) 增大参数可延缓但无法完全阻止可塑性丧失；4) 在稳态多语言训练下也存在可塑性丧失。

Conclusion: 即使是大规模Transformer语言模型，在经过足够长的训练后，无论是在持续学习还是稳态设置下，最终都会失去高效适应新数据的能力。

Abstract: The loss of plasticity - the ability of a network to learn new information after having already learned older information - is a fundamental challenge in creating artificial neural networks capable of continual learning. Although this phenomenon has been known for decades, it has mostly been studied in older, relatively small architectures and rarely in natural-language domains. To determine whether loss of plasticity remains a problem in the modern transformer-based LLM paradigm, we study plasticity loss in GPT-style Transformer models trained on a multilingual continual learning problem. Consistent with prior work, we find evidence of plasticity loss across models ranging from 5M to 314M non-embedding parameters, as measured by deterioration on a held-out Vietnamese probing task. We further find that the onset of plasticity loss follows a predictable scaling law, growing sublinearly with model size. These results suggest that larger models may delay the measurable effects of plasticity loss, but that increasing parameter count alone is likely to be insufficient to completely prevent it. We also find evidence of plasticity loss under stationary multilingual training, challenging the view that the phenomenon is exclusive to continual learning with abrupt task changes. Overall, our results suggest that even large Transformer language models trained on natural-language will eventually lose the ability to efficiently adapt to new data after sufficiently long training, in both continual and stationary settings.

### [249] [BluTrain: A C++/CUDA Framework for AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24780)
*Adhitya Charan,Adwaid Suresh,Anuj Kumar,Aparna A,Dhanakumar K,Dharun M S,Dinesh G,Goutham Kumar Reddy K,Harshini V M,Jenifa D,Jona Delcy C A,Kathirvel S,Killi Uma Maheswara Rao,Kiruthik Kanna M,Kurra Vishnu Sai,Madhumithaa G K,Navin Kumar,Ram Charan Golla,Revathi T,Rishikkanth R,Sanjay Krishna M,Surendra Vendra*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度学习进展更多取决于系统工程而非模型架构，现有框架（如PyTorch）存在系统复杂性高、硬件表达能力受限等问题，作者希望构建一个既能精确控制硬件表达、又能抽象系统复杂度的通用训练框架。

Method: 从第一性原理出发，使用标准C++和核心CUDA编程模型构建BluTrain。每个层均原生实现：带反向模式自动微分的类型化张量模块、线性代数库、缓存分配器、多模式分布式执行模块以及基于MLIR的深度学习编译器。

Result: 在8卡6000 Ada系统上训练124M参数的GPT-2（FP32），BluTrain平均吞吐量407K tokens/s（PyTorch为395K），内存占用减少22%，最终验证损失略低，数值精度严格保持一致。

Conclusion: BluTrain证明了从底层构建框架可以同时实现更高的吞吐量、更优的内存效率和严格的数值精度，且每一层都开放给原生调优，性能上限取决于框架自身的持续改进。

Abstract: Progress in deep learning is, at scale, more a matter of systems engineering than of modelling: the behaviour of a model in training (its throughput, its memory footprint, and the numerical fidelity of the result) is determined less by the architecture itself than by how that architecture is expressed on the hardware. To achieve absolute control over this hardware expression while abstracting away systems complexity to make modelling seamless and eliminating the need for repetitive orchestration logic, BluTrain was architected from first principles as a robust, lightweight, and architecture-general training framework in standard C++ and the core CUDA programming model. Every layer is implemented natively: a typed tensor module with reverse-mode autograd, a linear-algebra library, a caching allocator, a multi-mode distributed-execution module, and an MLIR-based deep-learning compiler. In formal evaluations training a 124M-parameter GPT-2 baseline in FP32 on an 8-GPU 6000 Ada system, BluTrain outperforms industry-standard baselines in both throughput (sustaining an average of 407K tokens/s versus PyTorch's 395K tokens/s) and memory efficiency (achieving up to a 22% footprint reduction), while strictly preserving numerical fidelity and converging to a marginally lower final validation loss. With every layer explicitly open to native tuning, the performance ceiling is the framework's own to raise.

### [250] [Assessing Distribution Shift in Human Activity Recognition for Domain Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24781)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然HAR领域已有诸多进展，但设备异构性和上下文变化导致的数据多样性问题仍是一大挑战。现有研究缺乏对不同类型分布偏移如何影响HAR模型以及由此引发的域泛化问题的系统性理解。

Method: 系统评估了4种分布偏移（设备类型、传感器位置、采样率、用户行为）的影响，量化其效应；建立统一的基于HAR的分布偏移基准，全面评估多达28种域泛化方法。

Abstract: While the field of Human Activity Recognition (HAR) continues to draw interest from researchers and advance in important ways, some key challenges remain. One of the most difficult aspects of building HAR models that show good performance in real-world settings is dealing with data diversity from device and sensor heterogeneity, and contextual changes that are intrinsic to real-world applications. While data diversity in HAR has been well-acknowledged in the literature, there remains a gap in understanding the effect of various types of distribution shifts on HAR models and the domain generalization problem that arises. Towards that end, this paper systematically evaluates 4 different types of distribution shifts, including variations in device type, sensor placement, sampling rate, and user behavior. Quantifying their effects, we illustrate that diversity shifts predominantly define all types of shifts, indicating the existence of unique features that are not shared across different domains. We then introduce a uniform HAR-based distribution shift benchmarks and conduct a comprehensive evaluation of up to 28 domain generalization methods. Our analysis exposes the limitations of current domain generalization algorithms in achieving model generalizability, marginally outperforming the empirical risk minimization baseline. This work represents the first systematic exploration of domain generalization and adaptation concerning specific distribution shifts in sensor-based HAR, offering an open-source benchmark platform and datasets to spur further research.

</details>


### [251] [Solving Inverse Problems of Chaotic Systems with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24824)
*Peiyan Hu,Jian Zhang,Jiashu Pan,Ruiqi Feng,Tao Zhang,Zhi-Ming Ma,Yuan-Sen Ting,Gongjie Li,Tailin Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出双向条件流匹配（Bi-CFM）方法解决混沌动力学中的逆问题（从最终状态推断初始条件），并针对守恒系统扩展为守恒约束Bi-CFM（CBi-CFM）。在Lorenz、电路、Lorenz 96及三体行星散射等系统中，该方法在五个分布级指标上超越基线，速度提升两个数量级以上；在真实球状星团观测中取得精度突破，为长时标混沌动力学的逆问题提供了可扩展的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌系统的建模至关重要但极具挑战，其逆问题（从最终状态推断初始条件）由于病态性、非唯一性、不稳定性以及潜在的时间反向混沌动力学而长期未解。

Method: 提出双向条件流匹配（Bi-CFM），学习初始状态与最终状态分布之间的双向映射，捕捉混沌演化的随机性并缓解指数级误差累积；针对具有守恒律的系统，进一步提出守恒约束双向条件流匹配（CBi-CFM）。

Result: 在经典Lorenz、电路、高维Lorenz 96系统中，Bi-CFM在五个分布级指标上超越基线，速度提升两个数量级以上；在三体行星散射中，CBi-CFM更好遵守守恒律，误差与真实值相当；在真实球状星团观测中取得精度突破。

Conclusion: 该方法为长时标真实世界混沌动力学的逆问题建立了一条可扩展的求解路径，代表了准确性的进步。

Abstract: Modeling chaotic systems is crucial yet challenging. Inverse problems in chaotic dynamics, namely inferring initial conditions from final states, remain largely unsolved because of ill-posedness, non-uniqueness, instability, and potentially chaotic time-reverse dynamics. We address this open problem with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching (Bi-CFM), which learns bidirectional mappings between distributions of initial and final states to capture the stochasticity of chaotic evolution and mitigate exponential error accumulation over time. Furthermore, for systems with conservation laws, we extend it to Conservation-constrained Bi-CFM (CBi-CFM). Across the classic Lorenz, Circuit, and high-dimensional Lorenz 96 systems, Bi-CFM improves five distribution-level metrics over baselines while achieving a speedup of more than two orders of magnitude. In the three-body planet-planet scattering problem in planetary dynamics, CBi-CFM better respects conservation laws, with conservation errors comparable to those of the ground truth. Finally, on real observations of globular clusters, collisional million-body systems shaped by $\sim 10^{10}$ years (10 Gyr) of evolution, our method represents an advance in accuracy, establishing a scalable route to solving inverse problems of long-timescale real-world chaotic dynamics.

</details>


### [252] [Difference-Making without Making a Difference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24832)
*Sander Beckers*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文证明Andreas & Günther的七个因果定义（包括最新的事实差异制造定义）实际上都同时体现了事实差异制造、反事实差异制造和基于规律性三种类型，表明这些分类并无实质区别。进一步比较发现，这一缺陷削弱了他们所有七个因果理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在揭示Andreas & Günther提出的七种实际因果定义及其分类体系存在问题，证明他们声称的三种不同类型（事实差异制造、反事实差异制造、基于规律性）实际上并非真正的区分。

Method: 作者通过分析Andreas & Günther最新（第七个）的事实差异制造定义，证明该定义同时包含了所有三种类型；随后将该新定义与其他六个定义在关键案例上进行对比分析。

Result: 发现Andreas & Günther最新的事实差异制造定义实际上融合了三种不同类型的因果定义，说明这些分类"没有区别的区别"；这一发现进一步动摇了他们全部七个因果理论的有效性。

Conclusion: Andreas & Günther的七个因果定义以及三类分类体系存在根本性缺陷，无法真正区分不同的因果关系类型。

Abstract: Over a series of seven papers, Andreas & Günther have introduced seven definitions of actual causation and have classified them as belonging to three different, competing, types of accounts: factual difference-making, counterfactual difference-making, and regularity-based. I show that their most recent - factual difference-making - definition instantiates all three types, thereby proving that these are distinctions without a difference. I further compare their novel account to the other six accounts on several crucial examples, revealing that this undermines all seven of their accounts.

### [253] [Accuracy and Satisfaction in Multi-Turn LLM Dialogues for NFR Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24834)
*Ali Pourghasemi Fatideh,Wilder Baldwin,Maria Dhakal,Collin McMillan,Sepideh Ghanavati*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究开发者与LLM对话助手（GitHub Copilot）在非功能需求（NFRs，以HIPAA合规为例）多轮对话中的准确性与质量。49名程序员评估148个NFRs后发现：开发者倾向于认同LLM的评估，但准确性较低；更长的系统回复和更多信息提供轮次反而降低用户满意度，而主动交互则提升满意度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM对话助手的评估基准仅关注功能正确性，忽视了非功能需求（NFRs）的评估。NFRs模糊、依赖上下文且涉及程序多个部分，需要多轮协作推理，而当前缺乏评估这种交互质量与准确性的方法。

Method: 招募49名程序员与GitHub Copilot交互，基于iTrust代码库评估148个HIPAA衍生的NFRs。从三个维度（需求满足程度、推理过程、代码定位）衡量，并对比开发者评估与专家标注的准确性，同时建模用户满意度的影响因素。

Result: 开发者倾向于同意LLM的评估，但准确性与专家标注相比很低；更长的系统回复和更多信息提供轮次负面影响用户满意度，而主动交互（proactive interactions）正面影响满意度。

Conclusion: 为设计支持NFR评估的LLM对话系统提供了实证见解：应减少冗长回复、避免过度信息灌输，增强主动交互能力。

Abstract: LLM-based dialogue assistants have become mainstream tools for software developers, yet current evaluation benchmarks focus exclusively on functional correctness. This leaves a critical gap in assessing the quality and accuracy of these conversations when handling Non-Functional Requirements (NFRs), which are inherently vague, context-dependent, and involve many parts of a program. Evaluating how well these systems support collaborative reasoning about NFRs requires methods that go beyond single-turn accuracy to capture both the correctness of the system's outputs and the quality of the multi-turn interaction. In this paper, we investigate the accuracy and quality of multi-turn conversations between developers and an LLM-based agent in the domain of Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) regulatory compliance. We hired 49 programmers to interact with GitHub Copilot to assess 148 HIPAA-derived NFRs against the iTrust codebase, a system designed to comply with HIPAA regulations, across three dimensions: requirement satisfaction level, reasoning, and code localization. We find that developers tend to agree with LLM assessments, but accuracy against expert ground truth is low. We model user satisfaction and find that longer system responses and more information-providing turns negatively affect user satisfaction, whereas proactive interactions positively affect it. Our findings provide insights for designing LLM-based dialogue systems that support NFR assessment.

### [254] [Grading the Grader: Lessons from Evaluating an Agentic Data Analysis System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24839)
*Tian Zheng,Kai-Tai Hsu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了多智能体数据分析系统LAMBDA在153个数值任务上的自动评估可靠性，提出三层人机级联评分策略（严格正则匹配、宽松LLM评分、片段人工审查），发现宽松评分器召回率达97%、严格评分器通过关键词提取召回率提升60个百分点，迭代提示机制使评分成功率从36%提升至97%，且变量类型是影响评分动态的最关键元数据字段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能数据分析系统输出复杂（代码、数值结果、文本诊断），传统单轮LLM评估方法难以适用，需要区分真正的输出偏差与评分工件的假象，因此研究如何可靠地自动化评估这类系统。

Method: 采用LAMBDA多智能体系统，在DSGym的153个QRData数值任务上，构建三层人机级联评分体系：严格正则匹配、基于LLM的宽松评分、片段式人工审查。引入关键词锚定提取pipeline和迭代提示机制（nudge），对比有无原始问题重新注入的效果。

Result: 两种自动评分器均达100%观察精度（0假阳性）；宽松评分器召回率97%；关键词提取使严格评分器召回率比末位数字启发式提升60个百分点；迭代提示将评分运行成功率从36%提升至97%，宽松通过率从16%提升至46%；重新注入原始问题无额外收益；变量类型是最关键的元数据字段。

Conclusion: 结合非GenAI和GenAI策略的级联评分体系能有效评估复杂数据分析系统；迭代提示作为答案模板线索有效；变量类型是影响评分动态的核心因素；后续可从更多元数据和任务类型扩展研究。

Abstract: Agentic data analysis systems produce rich outputs, including code, numerical results, and verbal diagnostics. This makes them more challenging to evaluate than single-turn LLM responses. It is therefore necessary to distinguish genuine disagreement between an agent's output and a ground-truth answer from grading artifacts. We investigate how reliably automated graders assess such a system and what strategies improve grading quality by applying LAMBDA, a multi-agent data-analysis system, on 153 numerical QRData tasks from DSGym. We develop and evaluate a three-layer human-AI grading cascade: strict regex matching, LLM-based lenient grading, and snippet-based human inspection, which combines non-GenAI and GenAI strategies with different failure profiles. Both automated graders achieve 100% observed precision (0/70 false positives). The lenient grader's recall is 97% against human labels. A keyword-anchored extraction pipeline raises the strict grader's recall by 60 percentage points over a last-number heuristic; the lenient grader is architecturally parser-independent. An iterative nudge mechanism raises grading run success from 36% to 97% and lenient-pass rates from 16% to 46%; comparing nudging with and without original-question re-injection shows that re-injection offers no benefit, confirming the nudge as an answer template cue. We further observe in this case study that variable type is the task metadata field most consistently associated with grading pipeline dynamics and observed outcome grades.

*Ahmad Pouramini,Hesham Faili*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出MTO框架，通过匹配预训练目标与下游任务目标，在生成和问答任务中实现超过120%的性能提升，尤其在少样本场景下表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同的预训练目标对编码器-解码器模型在下游任务（生成、问答、常识知识检索与补全）中的影响，并希望找到自动化的方法来匹配任务与最合适的训练目标。

Method: 提出Match Task to Objective (MTO)框架，包含：1) 自动化方法确定任务对应的预训练目标；2) 基于此目标的无监督数据准备方法；3) 与预训练/适应阶段目标对齐的微调模板设计；4) 扩展到提示调优方法中。

Result: 在少样本场景下相比传统方法性能提升超过120%；显著优于相关少样本工作；在完整数据集场景下也超越基线；同时增强了提示调优的性能。

Abstract: Prompt-based learning has emerged as a dominant paradigm in natural language processing. This study explores the impact of diverse pre-training objectives on the performance of encoder-decoder pre-trained language models across generation and question answering tasks, with a focus on commonsense knowledge retrieval and completion. We highlight the benefits of incorporating multiple objectives during both pre-training and fine-tuning stages. We introduce the Match Task to Objective (MTO) framework and methods for determining the appropriate objective for a given task. This framework offers automated methods to prepare task-related data for adaptation through unsupervised training, based on the identified objective. In the fine-tuning stage, we design novel templates that align with the objectives of the pre-training and adaptation stages. When aligned with task requirements, these strategies can achieve a performance gain of over 120\% compared to conventional methods in few-shot settings. They significantly outperform related works in few-shot settings and exceed the baseline even in full-dataset scenarios. Furthermore, we extend this approach to include prompt-tuning methodologies, providing guidance for more effective soft prompt engineering and optimization. Our strategies significantly enhance prompt-tuning performance as well. These insights hold substantial value, precisely guiding the selection and optimization of models customized for specific tasks. Code is available at https://github.com/puraminy/MTO/

### [256] [World Models in Pieces: Structural Certification for General Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24842)
*Yikai Lu,Yifei Wu,Xinyu Lu,Tongxin Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出结构认证（structural certification）框架，证明通用智能体无法实现通用能力，转而通过局部过渡分析为智能体的世界模型提供逐项保证，并给出算法实现O(1/n)+O(δ)误差界的紧界证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大世界（big-world）场景下，智能体能力必然专业化且碎片化，标准均匀保证无法区分关键瓶颈与无关失败，因此需要新的认证框架。

Method: 1) 形式化证明通用智能体不具普遍性；2) 提出结构认证框架，将带目标的条件性能映射为世界模型的逐项保证；3) 设计算法利用深度组合目标过滤特定转移，并给出误差界证明及紧性分析。

Result: 证明通用智能体在深度组合目标上具有结构化的世界模型，误差界为O(1/n)+O(δ)；该界在小区间δ下是紧的，且存在性由认证明确保证。

Conclusion: 结构认证框架能够定位长程规划可靠的特定转移，从而支持通用智能体的可认证部署。

Abstract: In the big-world regime, agents cannot be universally capable and their ability is inevitably specialized across a world model in pieces. Consequently, standard uniform guarantees fail to distinguish between the understanding of critical bottlenecks and irrelevant failures. We first formalize this limitation by proving that general agents are not universal, rendering standard worst-case analysis uninformative. To overcome this, we introduce structural certification, a transition-local framework that maps bounded goal-conditioned performance to entry-wise guarantees on the agent's internal world model. Our main contribution is constructive. We provide algorithms that filter specific transitions using deep compositional goals and prove that a general agent on these goals has a structural world model with a $\mathcal{O}(1/n) + \mathcal{O}(δ)$ error bound. Conversely, this bound is tight in the small-$δ$ regime, whose existence is explicitly guaranteed by our certification. These results enable the certifiable deployment of general agents by localizing the specific transitions where long-horizon planning is reliable.

</details>

*Negin Raoof,Richard Zhuang,Marianna Nezhurina,Etash Guha,Atula Tejaswi,Ryan Marten,Charlie F. Ruan,Tyler Griggs,Alexander Glenn Shaw,Hritik Bansal,E. Kelly Buchanan,Artem Gazizov,Reinhard Heckel,Chinmay Hegde,Sankalp Jajee,Daanish Khazi,Emmanouil Koukoumidis,Xiangyi Li,Hange Liu,Shlok Natarajan,Harsh Raj,Nicholas Roberts,Ethan Shen,Nishad Singhi,Michael Siu,Ashima Suvarna,Hanwen Xing,Patrick Yubeaton,Robert Zhang,Leon Liangyu Chen,Xiaokun Chen,Steven Dillmann,Saadia Gabriel,Xunyi Jiang,Anurag Kashyap,Boxuan Li,Yein Park,Minh Pham,Sujay Sanghavi,Lin Shi,Ke Sun,Yixin Wang,Zhiwei Xu,Erica Zhang,Siyan Zhao,Wanjia Zhao,Jenia Jitsev,Alex Dimakis,Benjamin Feuer,Ludwig Schmidt*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在7个智能体基准上平均准确率44.8%，比现有最强开源模型Nemotron-Terminal-32B（40.9%）提升3.9个百分点。训练数据在计算量受控下，在各个训练集规模上均优于其他开源数据集，表现出强扩展性。

Conclusion: 开源了训练集、数据处理流水线、实验数据和模型，为未来智能体模型训练的开源研究提供支持。

Abstract: Agentic language models dramatically expand the applications of AI yet little is publicly known about how to curate training data for broadly capable agents. Existing open efforts such as SWE-Smith, SERA, and Nemotron-Terminal typically target a single benchmark, leaving open the question of how to train models that generalize across diverse agentic tasks. The OpenThoughts-Agent (OT-Agent) project addresses this gap with a fully open data curation pipeline for training agentic models. We conduct more than 100 controlled ablation experiments to systematically investigate each stage of the pipeline, yielding insights on the importance of task sources and diversity. We then assemble a training set of 100K examples from our pipeline and fine-tune Qwen3-32B on this dataset, which yields an average accuracy of 44.8% across seven agentic benchmarks and a 3.9 percentage point improvement over the strongest existing open data agentic model (Nemotron-Terminal-32B, 40.9%). Moreover, our training data exhibits strong scaling properties, outperforming alternative open datasets at every training set size in compute-controlled comparisons. We publicly release our training sets, data pipeline, experimental data, and models at openthoughts.ai to support future open research on agentic model training.

### [258] [Beyond the Autoregressive Horizon: A Comprehensive Survey of Diffusion Models, World Modelling, and State Space Models for Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23690)
*Kishan Maharaj,Ashita Saxena,Srikanth Tamilselvam*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文批判了自回归语言模型在代码推理中的结构性局限（如缺乏全局规划、长程依赖弱、缺乏执行语义），并探讨了扩散模型、代码世界模型、状态空间模型等新兴范式作为突破方向，结合认知神经科学提出向"系统2"代码生成智能体发展的路线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自回归语言模型在代码生成中虽取得显著进展，但其逐词预测的本质限制了全局规划能力、长程依赖保持能力以及程序执行语义的接地性，亟需探索能突破这些瓶颈的新架构范式。

Method: 本文不提出新模型，而是综述三类新兴架构：①扩散模型——通过整体去噪生成代码，捕获长程句法约束；②代码世界模型——模拟执行状态以支持代码推理；③状态空间模型——提供线性时间复杂度的高效长上下文处理。并引入认知神经科学的"系统1/系统2"理论，提出未来方向。

Result: 文章指出AR模型在逻辑推理和扩展性方面的瓶颈，并论证了扩散模型、CWM、SSM等范式在克服这些局限上的潜力，同时提出"系统2"代码生成智能体的概念。

Conclusion: 为了突破当前代码智能的瓶颈，研究界应超越自回归范式的垄断，探索扩散模型、代码世界模型和状态空间模型等新方向，并借鉴认知科学构建具备深层推理能力的"系统2"代码生成智能体。

Abstract: Autoregressive (AR) language models have driven significant progress in automated software engineering, enabling powerful code generation and assistance systems. However, the next-token prediction paradigm introduces structural limitations for code reasoning, including restricted global planning, challenges in maintaining long-range dependencies, and limited grounding in program execution semantics. Noting the heavy skewness of existing literature towards AR models, we discuss emerging paradigms that could potentially overcome the logic and scaling bottlenecks of next-token prediction by unlocking next-generation architectural capabilities for code intelligence. Specifically, we discuss the potential of Diffusion Models, which generate code via holistic denoising that captures long-range syntactic constraints often missed by AR models. We also discuss Code World Models (CWMs), which simulate execution states to support reasoning, and State Space Models (SSMs), which provide linear-time efficiency for massive contexts. By connecting these developments with findings from cognitive neuroscience, we outline directions for developing "System 2" code generation agents.

### [259] [From Heuristics to Transformers: A Comprehensive Survey of Type Inference from Stripped Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23692)
*Hua Zheng,Yuhang Guo,Kuanishbay Sadatdiynov,Cheng Wen,Muhammad Sadiq,Dugang Liu,Jawwad Ahmed Shamsi,Anam Qureshi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了从无符号二进制文件中恢复高级类型信息的技术演化，涵盖从早期基于规则的启发式方法到现代深度学习架构（如Transformer和GNN），并指出了当前挑战与未来方向。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从剥离符号信息的二进制文件中恢复类型信息是逆向工程、漏洞分析和反编译的核心任务，然而该领域缺乏系统性的综述研究。

Method: 通过梳理二进制类型推断技术的发展脉络，将方法分为三个阶段：早期基于规则和约束求解（如BITY、BinSub）、上下文感知的神经模型（如EKLAVYA、CATI），以及当前基于Transformer和图神经网络（GNN）的架构（如SeeType、TYGR）。

Result: 识别出两大核心挑战：优化导致的语义损失（optimization-induced semantics loss）和结构类型恢复（structural type recovery）。

Conclusion: 未来研究方向应聚焦于神经符号推理（neuro-symbolic inference）以融合深度学习的灵活性与符号推理的可解释性。

Abstract: The recovery of high-level type information from stripped binaries-executables devoid of symbol tables and debugging information-is a cornerstone of software reverse engineering, vulnerability analysis, and decompilation. This survey tracks the evolution of binary type inference from early rule-based heuristics and static analysis to modern deep learning architectures. We analyze the shift from "duck typing" and constraint-solving techniques (e.g., BITY, BinSub) to context-aware neural models (e.g., EKLAVYA, CATI) and finally to state-of-the-art Transformer and Graph Neural Network (GNN) architectures (e.g., SeeType, TYGR). We identify core challenges, including optimization-induced semantics loss and structural type recovery, and propose future research directions in neuro-symbolic inference.

</details>


### [260] [Privacy Engineering: A Systematic Literature Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23696)
*Nemania Borovits,Damian Andrew Tamburri,Willem-Jan van den Heuvel*

TL;DR: 本文通过系统性综述90篇（2018-2025）关于GDPR隐私义务的软件工程研究，识别出13个维度构成的两个核心集群（PETs/PM/VT与GA/TC/OM）及其中介MS，绘制了生命周期映射和领域权重分布，为隐私工程提供了实用图谱和可复现的评估框架。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用系统性文献综述方法，综合2018至2025年间90项研究，通过主题综合（thematic synthesis）提取并归纳隐私工程的13个维度及其结构关系。

Result: 识别出两个核心集群：①隐私增强技术（PETs）、隐私度量（PM）与验证测试（VT）；②治理与问责（GA）、透明度与沟通（TC）与组织措施（OM）。建模与规范（MS）作为中介。生命周期映射显示不同阶段侧重不同维度。领域（医疗、IoT、Web测量、AI/ML）会重新加权但不改变整体结构。IRM、LM和DMPL作为主要焦点的研究较少。

Conclusion: 研究结果为隐私工程提供了实用地图和可复现的评估与更新支架，指出了未来研究重点方向。

Abstract: Privacy obligations under GDPR increasingly shape software engineering. We synthesize 90 studies from 2018 to 2025 using a systematic review with thematic synthesis to chart privacy engineering. Thirteen dimensions form two recurrent cores: Privacy Enhancing Technologies (PETs) with Privacy Metrics (PM) and Verification and Testing (VT) and Governance and Accountability (GA) with Transparency and Communication (TC) and Organizational Measures (OM). Modeling and Specification (MS) mediates between the cores. Lifecycle mapping shows concentrations at requirements and design (MS, GA), at implementation and verification (PETs, VT, PM, TC) and at operation and decommissioning (GA, OM, Data Subject Rights Management (DSRM), Incident Response and Management (IRM), Lifelong Management (LM)). Handoffs link models to rules and tests, mechanisms to metrics and deployments such as enclaves and ledgers to governance records. Domains reweight but do not alter structure: healthcare weights GA with VT and PETs, IoT and edge weight PETs with VT and PM at device and edge, web measurement weights TC with VT, AI and ML weight PETs with PM. IRM, LM and Data Minimization and Purpose Limitation (DMPL) are less often primary foci, signaling priorities for future work. The results provide a practical map and a replication-ready scaffold for assessment and updates.

### [261] [SemChunk-C: Semantic Segmentation for C Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23697)
*Boris Nazarov,Darya Frolova,Shaked Leibzirer,Pavel Kisilev*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出SemChunk-C，一系列轻量级语言模型（17M-150M参数），用于C家族语言代码的语义分块。该方法通过LLM分类器识别代码块边界并分配语义类别，在准确性和语义连贯性上匹配甚至超越基于更大LLM的分块器，并提升下游任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: C家族语言因复杂语法、宏展开和不规则结构模式，现有分块方法（固定窗口、启发式分割、语法工具）难以捕获有意义的函数单元，限制了检索和LLM下游任务的效能。

Method: 1) 定义一组代码块类别；2) 训练基于LLM的分类器，用于识别块边界并为每个块分配描述性功能属性；3) 基于前四个Ettin编码器（17M/32M/68M/150M参数）构建SemChunk-C系列轻量级模型，实现语义分块。

Result: 在多个数据集上达到高边界准确率和语义连贯性，匹配或超越基于更大代码LLM的分块器；在精选基准上验证了下游任务的性能提升。

Conclusion: 轻量级模型也能有效实现C家族代码的语义分块，适应嵌套定义和宏等复杂结构，为代码理解与检索提供实用方案。

Abstract: Semantic segmentation of code written in a C-family language remains a challenging problem, due to the language's complex syntax, macro expansion, and irregular structural patterns. Existing chunking methods, such as fixed-sized windows, heuristic splitting, and syntax-based tools, often fail to capture meaningful functional units, limiting the efficacy of retrieval and other downstream LLM driven tasks.
  In this paper, we address the problem of chunking in C-related languages. First, we define a set of code chunk categories. Second, we train an LLM-based classifier to a) identify chunk boundaries, and b) assign each chunk a descriptive functional attribute (a category), which can be useful for downstream tasks. By leveraging the LLM's ability to capture semantic context within the code, we assume flexible chunk boundaries, allowing to adapt to the specific structure and context of each instance. Third, we introduce SemChunk-C, a family of lightweight language models for semantic chunking of C-related files (.c, .cpp, .h, .cs, etc.). These models are based on the first four Ettin encoders [1] with 17M, 32M, 68M, and 150M parameters. Despite their relatively small size, they are capable of identifying cohesive code units, such as data structures, interface blocks, and other components. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our approach on real-world code, including challenging constructs such as nested definitions and macros.
  We test our approach on various datasets, and show that it achieves high boundary accuracy and semantic coherence, matching or outperforming chunkers that are based on much larger code-oriented LLMs. We also validate the improved performance of the downstream tasks on a few curated benchmarks.

### [263] [ESAA-Conversational: An Event-Sourced Memory Layer for Continuity, Handoff, and Curation Across Heterogeneous LLM Coding Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23752)
*Elzo Brito dos Santos Filho*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出ESAA-Conversational，一种基于事件溯源架构的领域特化方法，用于解决多LLM编码代理间会话状态漂移问题。该方法将可见对话视为本地事件存储，通过钩子捕获对话轮次，规范化写入只追加的activity.jsonl，并投影出handoff.md、state.md等只读模型。公共v1.1.0版本实现了PowerShell CLI，支持异构代理通过共享日志协作，无需直接代理间通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者越来越多地在多个LLM编码代理（如Codex、Grok、Claude Code）之间切换工作，但每个代理将其对话持久化在私有的、供应商特定的日志中，导致会话状态漂移——一个代理建立的目标、决策、待处理任务和理由在另一个代理接手时无法可靠获取。

Method: 将可见对话作为本地事件存储处理：通过钩子和监视器捕获可见对话轮次，规范化为只追加的activity.jsonl文件；通过确定性投影生成handoff.md、state.md、decisions.md、tasks.json等只读模型。机械捕获无需LLM推理，代理仅在显式策划时使用判断力。实现了PowerShell CLI，包含init、enable-hooks、sync、project、verify、context、decide、task等命令。

Result: 通过一个包含570个开发实验室事件的自参考案例研究表明，异构代理可以通过共享日志协作，无需直接的代理间通信通道。公共发行版排除了私有对话历史，保护了隐私。

Conclusion: ESAA-Conversational为多LLM代理协作中的会话状态漂移问题提供了一种实用解决方案，通过事件溯源方法实现跨异构代理的共享会话记忆，同时保持隐私保护。

Abstract: Software developers increasingly work with multiple LLM coding agents, switching among tools such as Codex, Grok, Claude Code, and other assistants as context windows fill, sessions end, or a particular agent becomes better suited to a subtask. Each agent, however, persists its conversation in a private and vendor-specific log. The result is conversational state drift: goals, decisions, open tasks, and rationales established with one agent are not reliably available when another agent takes over. This paper presents \emph{ESAA-Conversational}, a domain specialization of Event-Sourcing Agent Architecture (ESAA)~\cite{esaa} for shared conversational memory across heterogeneous agents. The method treats the visible conversation as a local event store: hooks and watchers capture visible turns, normalize them into an append-only \texttt{activity.jsonl}, and deterministically project read models such as \texttt{handoff.md}, \texttt{state.md}, \texttt{decisions.md}, and \texttt{tasks.json}. Mechanical capture does not require LLM inference; agents use judgment only for explicit curation, recording durable decisions and conversational tasks through domain commands. The public v1.1.0 release implements a PowerShell CLI with \texttt{init}, \texttt{enable-hooks}, \texttt{sync}, \texttt{project}, \texttt{verify}, \texttt{context}, \texttt{decide}, and \texttt{task}; includes \texttt{workspace\_root} isolation and a write-path lockfile; and is distributed as a greenfield package with an empty public log. A self-referential case study with 570 development-lab events shows that heterogeneous agents can collaborate through a shared log without a direct agent-to-agent channel, while the public distribution preserves privacy by excluding the private conversational history.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将目标、任务框架、生命周期状态、失效规则和恢复合约设计为一等运行时对象，委托有界执行给图运行时、智能体、工具或API，不替代简单流程中的工作流图。

Result: 形式化定义了问题，提出了运行时对象和架构选择标准，将评估框架作为未来实证验证的议程而非当前性能声明。

Abstract: Graph and multi-agent orchestration frameworks make production large language model (LLM) workflows practical, but they do not by themselves solve conversational continuity when users maintain several interdependent objectives. This conceptual systems paper focuses on the high-complexity end of that design space, where goals can be suspended, resumed, revised, and invalidated by actions in other goals. We introduce the Goal-Oriented Dialogue Runtime (GODR), a framework-neutral design pattern that treats goals, task frames, lifecycle state, invalidation rules, and resumption contracts as first-class runtime objects while delegating bounded execution to graph runtimes, agents, tools, or application programming interfaces (APIs). GODR is not proposed as a replacement for workflow graphs in simple guided processes; it is intended for complex, multi-domain, interruptible conversations where objective continuity cannot be recovered reliably from agent identity, chat history, or execution-graph position alone. The paper formalizes the problem, proposes runtime objects and architecture-selection criteria, and frames evaluation as an agenda for future empirical validation rather than as a measured performance claim.

Motivation: 大语言模型使研究生产变得可规模化，但瓶颈从产出人工制品转向评判研究主张。现有的自动化流程难以有效区分哪些环节可以机器验证、哪些需要人类判断，缺乏一个系统化的研究编排框架来解决这一问题。

Method: 提出了Agon研究编排器，基于六项设计原则（提示经济性、面向未来、最小提示、跨学科、大规模并行、零编码），通过Prompt Economy循环迭代运行，将可验证的流程自动化处理，剩余判断留给人类科学家。

Result: Agon在多个领域进行了444次Prompt Economy循环迭代部署，仅使用小型起始主题且无需人工编写实验代码。实验证明了系统的可扩展性，同时暴露了新类别的失败模式。作者将这些失败按严重性、可修复性、可见性和能力位置四个维度进行了分类整理。

Conclusion: Agon推动研究进入"机器规模化，人类掌舵"的新范式。失败分类法有效区分了循环可以自主发现并修复的失败与需要人类判断的失败，为未来人机协作的研究自动化系统提供了设计指导。

Abstract: Large language models are making research production scalable, shifting the bottleneck from producing artifacts to judging claims. We present \textsc{Agon}, a research orchestrator that validates what can be checked inside the workflow and leaves the remaining judgments to human scientists. \textsc{Agon} is built on six design principles: Prompt Economy, Future-Facing, Minimal Prompts, OmniDisciplinary, Massive Parallelism, and Zero-Code. We ran \textsc{Agon} across domains for 444 iterations of Prompt Economy loops, using only small starting topics and no human-written experimental code. These deployments demonstrate scalability while exposing new classes of failure. We organize these failures into a taxonomy along severity, fixability, visibility, and capability locus. The taxonomy separates failures the loops can see and fix from those that require human judgment. Together, these results show that \textsc{Agon} is pushing research toward a new paradigm: machine scales, human steers.

</details>


### [269] [AutoSpec: Safety Rule Evolution for LLM Agents via Inductive Logic Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24245)
*Pingchuan Ma,Zhaoyu Wang,Zimo Ji,Yuguang Zhou,Zhantong Xue,Zongjie Li,Shuai Wang,Xiaoqin Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AutoSpec是一个利用归纳逻辑编程（ILP）引导的反例驱动归纳合成（CEGIS）框架，能自动从用户标注中进化专家设计的安全规则，在代码执行和具身智能体领域将F1分数提升至0.98和0.93，同时保持规则可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体安全方法存在根本性权衡：手工规则可解释但脆弱（要么误报率高，要么漏报率高），神经分类器则缺乏可解释性。需要一种既能自动优化规则、又能保持可解释性的方法。

Method: AutoSpec采用ILP引导的CEGIS框架：从专家规则开始，迭代评估规则并挖掘假阳性和假阴性反例；利用ILP学习区分两类反例的谓词，大幅剪枝规则编辑的指数级搜索空间；生成候选规则编辑并验证，直至收敛。

Result: 在291个执行轨迹（代码执行+具身智能体）上，规则F1达到0.98和0.93；假阳性降低高达94%同时保持高召回率；4-5次迭代内收敛；ILP引导方法比启发式CEGIS的F1高4.8倍；学到的规则可读、可审计且能泛化。

Conclusion: AutoSpec证明了通过ILP引导的规则进化可以有效解决LLM智能体安全中可解释性与自动化的权衡，产出兼顾精确率和召回率的可解释安全规则。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly automate complex tasks by integrating language models with external tools and environments. However, their autonomy poses significant safety risks: agents may execute destructive commands, leak sensitive data, or violate domain constraints. Existing safety approaches face a fundamental tradeoff: hand-crafted rules are interpretable but brittle, with overly conservative rules blocking safe operations (high false positives) while permissive rules miss unsafe behaviors (high false negatives). Neural classifiers lack the interpretability required for safety-critical deployments.
  We present AutoSpec, a framework that automatically evolves deployed expert-designed safety rules from user safe/unsafe annotations through counterexample-guided inductive synthesis (CEGIS) guided by inductive logic programming (ILP). Starting from the expert rules and a stream of annotated traces, AutoSpec iteratively evaluates rules, mines false-positive and false-negative counterexamples, uses ILP to learn which predicates discriminate them, generates candidate rule edits, and verifies candidates to select the best revision. The key insight is that ILP efficiently identifies predicates that appear frequently in false negatives but rarely in false positives (or vice versa), dramatically pruning the exponential search space of rule edits. This continues until convergence, producing interpretable rules that balance precision and recall.
  We evaluate AutoSpec on 291 execution traces spanning code execution and embodied agent domains. AutoSpec raises rule F1 to 0.98 and 0.93 across the two domains, achieving up to 94% false positive reduction while maintaining high recall, and converges within 4-5 iterations. The ILP-guided approach achieves up to 4.8x higher F1 than heuristic CEGIS. The learned rules are human-readable, auditable, and generalize to unseen scenarios.

</details>

From the SOA perspective, architectural decisions need to be made by performing a trade-off analysis and providing quantitative guarantees of system configurations under prescribed levels of uncertainty. Abstract: Generative AI coding agents are entering the open-source supply chain, yet their diverse and often invisible traces leave their prevalence poorly understood. No single method captures more than a fraction of activity: multi-method detection identifies 850,157 Claude Code commits in one snapshot, of which bot-account lookup_the signal most adoption studies rely on_recovers only 28,154 (3.3%), a 30x relative-recall gap, so single-signal prevalence estimates are biased low by at least this factor. Every detection pattern is hand-validated (495 labels) with per-cell precision and Wilson confidence intervals. Compared against an independent pull-request census (AIDev), the two channels capture nearly disjoint agent populations_a PR census misses 79% of commit-detected Claude Code adopters and essentially all Codex adopters_and different kinds of work: PR-deployed cloud agents (Codex, Cursor) surface as feature work, while commit-deployed in-editor agents (Claude Code, OpenHands, Aider) surface as maintenance. Method: 提出BigBag智能体框架，生成结构化的可执行修复转换程序（在API级别编码修复逻辑），可迁移到任何受相同更新影响的客户端项目。结合四种大语言模型和两种AST转换引擎（Spoon和JavaParser）进行实验。

Abstract: Modern software projects depend on third-party libraries that evolve continuously, introducing breaking API changes that prevent client code from compiling after a dependency update. When the same library update breaks multiple projects, existing repair approaches generate project-specific patches that cannot be reused, requiring each affected project to be repaired independently. We present BigBag, an agentic framework that generates fixing transformations: structured, executable programs that encode the repair logic at the API level and transfer to any client broken by the same update. We evaluate BigBag on 157 compilation failure breaking dependency updates from the BUMP benchmark, across eight configurations combining four large language models and two AST transformation engines (Spoon and JavaParser). The best configuration achieves a compilable transformation rate of 94.3% and a fix rate of 78.6%. Generated transformations transfer across projects, achieving a cross-project fix rate of 33.3% overall and 80% or above for breaking updates where all clients invoke the affected API element uniformly. These results show that agentic generation of reusable fixing transformations is a viable approach to scalable repair of breaking updates.

Abstract: When a core definition changes, every dependent artefact must be updated, a cascading problem central to software maintenance. In Model-Driven Engineering (MDE), the dominant two-level modelling (2LM) paradigm fragments domain knowledge across metamodel and model artefacts that must be kept mutually consistent, making co-evolution a persistent source of inconsistencies and effort. Multi-level modelling (MLM) unifies these artefacts and is claimed to reduce co-evolution burden, but this has not been tested in a controlled, paired comparison against 2LM. We hypothesise that MLM's structural unification yields fewer post-change inconsistencies and a smaller modification footprint than 2LM for semantically equivalent evolution scenarios. To test this, we present a pre-registered, mutation-based empirical comparison of co-evolution behaviour in both paradigms. From a curated corpus of published 2LM co-evolution scenarios, we construct semantically equivalent MLM counterparts, apply identical evolution mutations to both, and measure outcomes through automated consistency checking and pre-registered hypothesis tests. Positive controls and a blinded mapping protocol guard against bias. This design provides the first empirical framework for assessing whether paradigm-level structural choices affect cascading maintenance burden, operationalising co-evolution burden as two automatically measurable outcome variables and delivering a reusable benchmarking protocol for replication and extension.

*Pablo Valle,Shaukat Ali,Aitor Arrieta,Lionel Briand*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出MANGO，一个多智能体框架，能够从自然语言描述中自动生成细粒度测试预言（oracle），用于测试视觉-语言-动作（VLA）机器人系统，克服了传统手工构建预言成本高、可重用性差、仅提供最终状态评估等局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA机器人测试方法依赖手工构建的符号化测试预言，不仅构建成本高、依赖领域专家、与特定任务和环境强耦合导致可扩展性差，而且只能评估最终任务结果，无法提供中间行为和故障定位信息。

Method: MANGO框架包含三个步骤：1）从自然语言描述中生成可复用的原子任务库；2）为每个原子任务生成基于模拟器的预言定义；3）将复杂指令分解为有序的原子动作序列，生成可执行的细粒度预言。框架通过生成器（Generator）、评估器（Assessor）和裁判（Judge）三个智能体协作，以结构化反馈迭代优化生成结果。

Result: 在LIBERO_10和RoboCasa Humanoid Tabletop基准上的实验表明，MANGO生成的细粒度预言能检测到与符号化预言相当数量的故障，同时能准确定位故障并提供更丰富的诊断信息。消融实验进一步分析了各组件贡献和初始任务集的影响，同时保持了预言质量。

Conclusion: MANGO证明了为VLA机器人自动生成测试预言的可行性和有效性，为VLA机器人测试提供了更可扩展、更细粒度的解决方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are emerging robotic control systems that integrate perception, language understanding, and action generation in a unified architecture. Existing testing approaches for VLA-enabled robots rely on manually constructed symbolic test oracles that determine task success from final environment states. These oracles are costly to construct, require domain expertise, and are often tightly coupled to specific tasks and environments, limiting scalability and reuse. Furthermore, they provide only end-state assessments of task outcomes, offering limited insight into intermediate behavior and fault localization. To address these limitations, we introduce MANGO, a multi-agent framework that automatically generates fine-grained oracles from natural-language descriptions of robotic tasks. MANGO first generates a reusable library of atomic tasks, then generates simulator-grounded oracle definitions for each atomic task, and finally produces executable fine-grained oracles by decomposing complex instructions into ordered sequences of atomic actions and corresponding oracles. The framework uses collaborative Generator, Assessor, and Judge agents that iteratively refine generated artifacts through structured feedback. We evaluate MANGO on the LIBERO_10 and RoboCasa Humanoid Tabletop benchmarks. Results show that MANGO generates executable, fine-grained oracles that detect a similar number of failures as symbolic oracles while accurately localizing them and providing richer diagnostic information. Through ablation studies, we further analyzed component contributions and the effect of initial task set, while preserving oracle quality. Overall, the results show the feasibility and effectiveness of test oracle generation for VLA-enabled robots testing.

</details>

### [278] [Overconfident Coordinates: Quantifying Confidence in Traceroute Geolocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24027)
*Santiago Klein,Caleb J. Wang,Fabián E. Bustamante*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出路径一致性评分（PCS）框架，通过隐马尔可夫模型融合多源地理元数据与速度约束，对traceroute路径进行城市级地理定位一致性评估，在验证路径上94.2%的解码序列平均误差低于200公里。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有互联网路径地理定位方法依赖商业数据库、rDNS标签、Geofeeds等多源数据，但这些来源仅提供点位置信息，缺乏校准的可信度，研究者无法判断地理路径的可信程度。

Method: 将路径地理定位建模为序列一致性优化问题：利用隐马尔可夫模型（HMM）融合局部证据（多源地理元数据）与全局约束（光速限制、经验延迟先验），输出路径一致性评分；同时提出路径-模型对齐度量，比较解码路径与参考路径的光速残差增量。

Result: 在413,354条RIPE Atlas traceroute和6,555条经过主动探测验证的路径上，94.2%的解码序列平均误差低于200公里。PCS在不同商业数据库间中位数评分差异小于5%，而对齐度量显示DB-IP和IP2Location超过半数路径需大幅校正，IPinfo仅15%。

Conclusion: PCS提供了一种与具体地理数据库无关的路径级可信度量化方法，使下游分析能评估地理结论的置信度，而非不加限定地继承数据库精度。

Abstract: Studies of Internet paths often attach router locations to traceroute hops using commercial geolocation databases, rDNS labels, Geofeeds, and IXP metadata. These sources provide useful hints, but they report point locations without calibrated confidence, leaving researchers unable to tell whether a geographic path is trustworthy. We introduce Path Consistency Scoring (PCS), a passive framework that evaluates router geolocation as a path-level consistency problem. PCS models each traceroute as a sequence of candidate city-level locations and uses a Hidden Markov Model to fuse local evidence with speed-of-light constraints and empirical latency priors. PCS produces a path consistency score summarizing how well metadata and observed RTT increments support a coherent geographic interpretation. Because this score is only meaningful when latency proxies for geography, we also define a Path-Model Alignment metric that compares speed-of-light residual increments of the decoded path against a reference path. We evaluate on 413,354 RIPE Atlas traceroutes and a 6,555-path subset verified by active probing. On validated paths, 94.2% of decoded sequences achieve mean error below 200 km. PCS is largely GeoDB-agnostic; median scores vary by less than 5% across four commercial databases, while the alignment metric reveals that over half of DB-IP and IP2Location paths require substantial correction, compared with 15% for IPinfo. This lets downstream analyses quantify confidence in their geographic conclusions rather than inheriting database accuracy without qualification.

</details>


### [279] [SkyChain Intelligence: A Blockchain-Secured Multi-Agent DRL Framework for Low-Altitude Embodied Artificial Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24193)
*Haoxiang Luo,Tianqi Jiang,Ruichen Zhang,Yinqiu Liu,Gang Sun,Hongfang Yu,Abbas Jamalipour,Dong In Kim*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出SkyChain Intelligence框架，通过集成智能体AI、联盟区块链和多智能体深度强化学习（MADRL），解决低空经济网络中LAEAI代理在去中心化环境下面临的自主性、安全性和效率三难困境，实现了任务完成率94.1%、300训练轮次内稳定收敛的优异性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低空经济中资源受限的LAEAI代理在去中心化LACNet中面临自主性、安全性和效率的根本性三难困境，现有方案孤立地优化计算性能或增强安全性，未能解决不可信动态环境中信任、性能和开销之间的内在权衡。

Method: 提出SkyChain Intelligence框架，协同集成智能体AI、联盟区块链和MADRL。设计基于轻量级区块链的分散式信任管理系统（含动态声誉机制），开发混合动作空间MADDPG算法，将链上声誉分数嵌入奖励函数，联合优化卸载决策、资源分配和无人机3D轨迹。

Result: 在任务完成延迟和能耗方面优于最先进基线，基线场景下实现94.1%的任务完成率，并在300训练轮次内稳定收敛。

Conclusion: 为低空领域构建安全、自主、高效的机器对机器计算生态系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: With the rapid development of the Low-Altitude Economy (LAE) ecosystem, Low-Altitude Embodied Artificial Intelligence (LAEAI) agents have become the core carriers of autonomous aerial services, thereby enabling dynamic Low-altitude Computility Networks (LACNets) for distributed computing resource sharing. However, resource-constrained LAEAI agents in decentralized LACNets face a fundamental trilemma of autonomy, security, and efficiency. Existing solutions primarily focus on either optimizing computational performance or enhancing security in isolation, failing to address the inherent trade-offs among trust, performance, and overhead in untrusted dynamic environments with malicious agents. To tackle this challenge, this paper proposes SkyChain Intelligence, a holistic framework that synergistically integrates agentic AI, consortium blockchain, and Multi-Agent Deep Reinforcement Learning (MADRL). We design a lightweight blockchain-based decentralized trust management system with a dynamic reputation mechanism and develop a hybrid-action-space MADDPG algorithm that embeds on-chain reputation scores into the reward function to jointly optimize offloading decisions, resource allocation, and drone 3D trajectories. Extensive simulations demonstrate that our framework outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in task completion latency and energy consumption, while achieving a 94.1% task completion rate in the baseline scenario and stable convergence within 300 training episodes. This work provides a viable path for building secure, autonomous, and efficient machine-to-machine computing ecosystems in the low-altitude domain.

</details>


### [280] [FORESEE: A Cooperative Lane Change Model for Connected and Automated Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24201)
*Rafael Molina-Masegosa,Sergei S. Avedisov,Miguel Sepulcre,Javier Gozalvez,Yashar Z. Farid,Onur Altintas*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: FORESEE是一个基于V2X数据的协作换道模型，通过提前组织车辆按期望速度分道，实现更高效、更节能的换道，减少交通扰动并提升驾驶舒适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非协作换道仅依赖自车及邻近车辆的短期局部信息，导致交通流扰动大、速度波动明显、能效低下。本文旨在通过V2X数据实现协作换道，提前预判交通状况以优化换道决策。

Method: 利用V2X数据获取全局交通信息，按车辆期望速度进行车道组织，实现交通流均质化；通过预判交通状况提前规划并组织换道，减少不必要的换道次数。

Result: 相比非协作换道，FORESEE提升了平均车速和能效；车辆速度更接近期望速度，速度和加速度波动更小，驾驶舒适性提高；能更好地管理障碍物等道路扰动。

Conclusion: FORESEE为基于V2X的机动协调设计提供了有价值的框架，其有效性取决于换道方式及提前规划和组织机动能力。

Abstract: This paper presents FORESEE, a novel cooperative lane change model for connected and automated driving. FORESEE leverages Vehicle-to-Everything (V2X) data to anticipate traffic conditions and effectively organize lane changes. Specifically, it uses V2X data to organize vehicles into lanes based on their desired speeds, which helps to homogenize traffic flow and reduce disturbances caused by speed differences among vehicles within the same lane. The study demonstrates that implementing cooperative lane changes with FORESEE enhances average vehicle speed and energy efficiency compared to non-cooperative lane changes, which typically rely on short-term and local information about the ego vehicle and its immediate neighbors. This is achieved through fewer but more effective lane changes. Additionally, vehicles can maintain speeds closer to their desired speeds, resulting in fewer fluctuations in speed and acceleration and enhanced driving comfort. Moreover, cooperative lane changes can better manage road traffic disturbances, such as obstacles, by anticipating traffic conditions and organizing lane changes ahead. FORESEE serves as a valuable framework for the future design and testing of V2X-based maneuver coordinations as their effectiveness depends on how vehicles change lanes and their ability to plan and organize maneuvers in consideration of the upcoming traffic conditions.

</details>


### [281] [Importance of Intent-Sharing for V2X-based Maneuver Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24203)
*Rafael Molina-Masegosa,Sergei S. Avedisov,Miguel Sepulcre,Javier Gozalvez,Yashar Z. Farid,Onur Altintas*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究了意图共享（intent-sharing）对联网自动驾驶车辆（CAVs）协同机动的影响，通过量化成功协调比例，证明直接获取其他车辆驾驶意图（而非轨迹预测）能显著提升协调效果，强调应将意图共享纳入协同协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机动协调需要精确了解其他车辆的驾驶意图，而现有方法多依赖轨迹预测。研究者希望探究直接意图共享相比轨迹预测能否更有效提升协调成功率。

Method: 通过量化成功协调的比例，比较意图共享方法与基于当前运动学数据的轨迹预测方法在高速公路变道场景中的协调效果。

Result: 在两个场景中，直接获取附近车辆驾驶意图的意图共享方法在机动协调方面均实现了显著改进。

Conclusion: 意图共享能显著提升CAVs的机动协调有效性，应将其纳入机动协调协议中。

Abstract: This paper examines the critical role of intent-sharing in enabling effective maneuver coordination for connected and automated vehicles (CAVs). Successful maneuver coordinations require vehicles to accurately know other vehicles' driving intentions. Intent-sharing can be achieved by the remote vehicles directly communicating their plans with the ego vehicle, as opposed to the ego vehicle predicting the trajectory on the remote vehicles' behalf. In this paper, we investigate the potential of intent-sharing on maneuver coordination effectiveness by quantifying the percentage of successful coordinations. We analyze the potential of intent-sharing by comparing its effectiveness for coordinated lane changes in a highway scenario with the effectiveness of a trajectory prediction method based on current kinematic data. Our analysis demonstrates in two scenarios substantial improvements in maneuver coordination when CAVs have direct access to the nearby vehicles' driving intentions through intent sharing. These findings highlight the importance of including intent-sharing in the maneuver coordination protocol.

</details>


### [282] [BRAVR: An AP-Assisted Online DRL Mechanism for Interactive VR Bitrate Adaptation over Wi-Fi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24389)
*Miguel Casasnovas,Francesc Wilhelmi,Boris Bellalta*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出BRAVR，一种基于深度强化学习的去中心化VR比特率自适应机制，通过整合Wi-Fi接入点（AP）的网络层信息与应用层观测，在共享无线环境下优化视觉质量、保证流媒体性能并促进空中时间公平性。在真实VR流媒体系统和物理Wi-Fi测试平台上的实验表明，BRAVR在QoS保障、避免空中时间过利用等方面优于强启发式基线和无AP辅助的消融变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交互式VR流媒体在Wi-Fi上面临动态信道条件和共享介质竞争的挑战，实时比特率自适应极为困难，且终端对底层网络状况的可见性有限。现有方法未充分利用AP端可获取的无线网络统计信息来辅助决策。

Method: 将VR比特率自适应建模为网络感知的在线决策问题，提出基于深度强化学习的去中心化机制BRAVR，将应用层观测与AP端轻量级无线网络统计信息融合，辅助比特率自适应决策。

Result: 在真实VR流媒体系统和物理Wi-Fi测试平台上，BRAVR强于强启发式基线和无AP辅助的消融变体，实现了稳健的QoS，有效防止了空中时间过利用。

Conclusion: AP辅助的在线学习对去中心化交互式VR流媒体在商用Wi-Fi上的有效性得到验证，为共享无线环境下的比特率自适应提供了实用见解。

Abstract: Interactive virtual reality (VR) streaming over Wi-Fi requires stringent latency and reliability guarantees, which become increasingly difficult to achieve under dynamic channel conditions and shared medium contention. These challenges make real-time bitrate adaptation a critical yet fundamentally difficult control problem, particularly under limited visibility of the underlying network conditions. This paper formulates VR bitrate adaptation as a network-aware, online decision-making problem and proposes BRAVR, a decentralized deep reinforcement learning (DRL) mechanism designed to optimize visual quality while maintaining streaming performance and promoting airtime fairness in multi-user scenarios. BRAVR integrates application-layer observations with lightweight wireless network statistics collected at the Wi-Fi access point (AP) serving the VR client, enabling more informed bitrate adaptation decisions. We implement BRAVR in a real VR streaming system and evaluate it on a physical Wi-Fi testbed against a strong heuristic baseline and an ablated BRAVR variant without AP assistance. Experimental results show that BRAVR consistently achieves its design objectives, delivering robust quality of service (QoS) and preventing sustained airtime overutilization. It also outperforms its ablated counterpart, highlighting the benefits of incorporating network-level information into the bitrate adaptation control loop. Overall, these results demonstrate the effectiveness of AP-assisted online learning for decentralized interactive VR streaming over commodity Wi-Fi and provide practical insights into bitrate adaptation in shared wireless environments.

</details>


### [283] [Building a Low-cost Network Digital Twin for the IoT-Edge-Cloud Continuum Using Open-Source Tooling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24853)
*Josevany do Amaral,Rute C. Sofia*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于Containerlab、OVS、ONOS等开源工具构建的低成本网络数字孪生框架，用于IIoT边缘部署验证，在RTT中位数和UDP吞吐量上与物理环境高度吻合，并分析了TCP吞吐量和丢包差异的根因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不中断真实基础设施的前提下验证网络配置和测试故障场景是IoT-边缘-云环境中的开放运营挑战。

Method: 使用Containerlab进行容器原生拓扑仿真，Open vSwitch实现虚拟交换，ONOS实现SDN流量工程，Prometheus+Grafana进行实时遥测监控。

Result: 在RTT中位数上偏差仅0.4ms，UDP吞吐量偏差0.03Mbps；TCP吞吐量和丢包率存在可解释的虚拟化伪影差异。

Conclusion: 该低成本开源数字孪生框架能有效逼近物理网络行为，为边缘网络验证提供了可行方案，同时明确了虚拟化引入的差异及修复路径。

Abstract: Validating network configurations and testing failure scenarios in IoT-edge-cloud environments without disrupting live infrastructure remains an open operational challenge. This paper presents a low-cost, fully open-source Network Digital Twin (NDT) for IIoT edge deployments, built on Containerlab, Open vSwitch, ONOS, and a Prometheus+Grafana observability stack. The framework integrates container-native topology emulation, SDN-driven traffic engineering, and real-time telemetry in a single deployable artefact. Validation against a physical Raspberry Pi edge WLAN shows strong distributional convergence on RTT median (delta = 0.4 ms) and UDP throughput (delta = 0.03 Mbps). Remaining divergences on TCP throughput and packet loss are attributed to identifiable virtualisation artefacts, with root causes and remediation paths provided.

</details>
